<script>
	document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
		// ============================================================================
		// INITIALIZATION
		// ============================================================================
		const desktopFilterForm = document.querySelector('.desktop-filter-form');
		const tabletFilterForm = document.querySelector('.tablet-filter-form')
		const mobileFilterToggle = document.getElementById('mobileFilterToggle');
		const mobileFilterDrawer = document.getElementById('mobileFilterDrawer');
		const drawerBackdrop = document.getElementById('drawerBackdrop');
		const drawerClose = document.getElementById('drawerClose');
		const mobileFilterForm = document.getElementById('mobileFilterForm');
		const mobileCheckboxes = mobileFilterForm.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]');

		// ============================================================================
		// AUTO-SUBMIT FILTERS (DESKTOP & TABLET)
		// ============================================================================
		function addAutoSubmitToForm(form) {
			if (!form) return;

			const checkboxes = form.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]');
			checkboxes.forEach(function (checkbox) {
				checkbox.addEventListener('change', function () {
					// Add a small delay to allow the checkbox to update visually
					setTimeout(function () {
						form.submit();
					}, 100);
				});
			});
		}

		// ============================================================================
		// MOBILE DRAWER HANDLERS
		// ============================================================================

		function closeDrawer() {
			mobileFilterDrawer.classList.remove('drawer-open');
			document.body.style.overflow = ''; // Restore scroll
		}

		if (mobileFilterToggle) {
			mobileFilterToggle.addEventListener('click', function () {
				mobileFilterDrawer.classList.add('drawer-open');
				document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
			});
		}

		if (drawerBackdrop) {
			drawerBackdrop.addEventListener('click', closeDrawer);
		}

		if (drawerClose) {
			drawerClose.addEventListener('click', closeDrawer);
		}

		if (mobileFilterForm) {
			mobileFilterForm.addEventListener('submit', function () {
				setTimeout(closeDrawer, 100);
			});
		}

		mobileCheckboxes.forEach(function (checkbox) {
			checkbox.addEventListener('change', function (e) {
				e.stopPropagation();
			});
		});

		// ============================================================================
		// CATEGORY TOGGLE (VIEW ALL/LESS)
		// ============================================================================

		function setupCategoryToggle(containerSelector, btnSelector) {
			const container = document.querySelector(containerSelector);
			const btn = document.getElementById(btnSelector);

			if (!container || !btn) return;

			const options = container.querySelectorAll('.filter-option');

			// Hide toggle if 8 or fewer options
			if (options.length <= 8) {
				btn.style.display = 'none';
				return;
			}

			// Initialize as collapsed
			container.classList.add('collapsed');
			btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
			btn.classList.remove('expanded');

			btn.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
				e.preventDefault();

				const isExpanded = !container.classList.toggle('collapsed');
				btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', isExpanded ? 'true' : 'false');
				btn.classList.toggle('expanded', isExpanded);

				// Update button text
				const arrowSvg =
					'<svg class="arrow-down" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><polyline points="6,9 12,15 18,9"></polyline></svg>';
				btn.innerHTML = isExpanded ? `View less ${arrowSvg}` : `View all ${arrowSvg}`;
			});
		}

		// ============================================================================
		// INITIALIZE ALL FUNCTIONALITY
		// ============================================================================

		addAutoSubmitToForm(desktopFilterForm);
		addAutoSubmitToForm(tabletFilterForm);
		setupCategoryToggle('.categories-filter-options', 'categoriesViewAll');
		setupCategoryToggle('.categories-filter-options-tablet', 'categoriesViewAllTablet');
		setupCategoryToggle('.categories-filter-options-desktop', 'categoriesViewAllDesktop');
	});
</script>
    </main>

    <script>
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
            if (typeof MktoForms2 === 'undefined') return;

            MktoForms2.loadForm(
                "//pages.specterops.io",
                "205-XLL-990",
                1014,
                function(form) {
                    var formEl = form.getFormElem()[0];

                    // Remove all inline Marketo styles
                    destyleMktoForm(form);

                    // Override submit button text
                    
                    // On success: redirect or show thank-you message
                    form.onSuccess(function() {
                        var wrapper = document.getElementById('mktoForm_1014_wrapper');

                                                window.location.href = "https://specterops.io/confirmation/";
                        return false;
                                            });
                }
            );

            /**
             * Remove Marketo inline styles and disable injected style/link elements
             */
            function destyleMktoForm(mktoForm) {
                var formEl = mktoForm.getFormElem()[0];
                if (!formEl) return;

                var arrayify = Function.prototype.call.bind(Array.prototype.slice);

                var styledEls = arrayify(formEl.querySelectorAll('[style]')).concat([formEl]);
                styledEls.forEach(function(el) {
                    el.removeAttribute('style');
                });

                var styleTags = arrayify(formEl.querySelectorAll('style'));
                styleTags.forEach(function(tag) {
                    tag.parentNode.removeChild(tag);
                });

                var styleSheets = arrayify(document.styleSheets);
                styleSheets.forEach(function(ss) {
                    if (ss.ownerNode && formEl.contains(ss.ownerNode)) {
                        ss.disabled = true;
                    }
                });

                formEl.setAttribute('data-styles-ready', 'true');
            }

            // Ensure destyling runs if the form renders asynchronously
            MktoForms2.whenRendered(function(form) {
                destyleMktoForm(form);
            });
        });
    </script>
                </div>
                  </div>
      </div>
    </div>

        let $socialsWrapper = $('.socials-wrapper');
        if ($socialsWrapper.length) {
            let $socialLinks = $socialsWrapper.find('.so-btn');
            $socialLinks.each(function () {
                let $this = $(this);
                let href = $this.attr('href');
                let updatedHref = "https://slack.specterops.io";
                if (href === "https://join.slack.com/t/bloodhoundhq/shared_invite/zt-1tgq6ojd2-ixpx5nz9Wjtbhc3i8AVAWw") {
                    $this.attr('href', updatedHref);

    });

<!-- External Script : Temp Button Disable -->
<script type="text/javascript">
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
    const selectors = [
        "body.so-con .rs-general-cta-section a.btn",
        "body.so-con .rs-so-con-page-hero-section a.btn"
    ];

    selectors.forEach(selector => {
        document.querySelectorAll(selector).forEach(el => {
            // Remove unwanted attributes
            ["data-toggle", "data-target", "aria-label"].forEach(attr => {
                el.removeAttribute(attr);
            });

            // Force links to open in a new tab
            el.setAttribute("target", "_blank");
            el.setAttribute("rel", "noopener noreferrer"); // security best practice
        });
    });
});
</script>

           return function() {                var context = this, args = arguments;                var later = function() {                    timeout = null;                    if ( !immediate ) func.apply( context, args );                };                var callNow = immediate && !timeout;                clearTimeout( timeout );                timeout = setTimeout( later, wait );                if ( callNow ) func.apply( context, args );
